SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_09_FILE##4080290 COCA  A    0  259 According to the 2005 report of the GCIM , the factors that precipitate migration include : ( 1 ) wage disparities : 45.7% of people in Sub-Saharan Africa , 14.4% in South Asia , and 10.4% in Latin America and the Caribbean earn less than $1 per day ; ( 2 ) unemployment rates : 12.2% in the Middle East and North Africa , 10.9% in Sub-Saharan Africa , and 6.6% in industrialized economies ; ( 3 ) differentials in life expectancy : 58 years in low income countries , and 78 years in high income countries ; ( 4 ) education gaps : 58% women and 68% men literate in low income countries , almost full literacy in high income countries ; 76% primary school enrollment in low income countries , almost full enrollment in high income countries ; ( 5 ) demographic gradients : on average 5.4 children born to each woman in Sub-Saharan Africa , compared with 3.8 in the Arab World , 2.5 in Latin America and the Caribbean , World : New Directions for Action 84 , http : **57;69506;TOOLONG ( accessed May 2 , 2009 ) .
